## Instruction

There is a class schedule for the first semester of the 2025-26 academic year in the workspace. I want to take Natural Language Processing (自然语言处理) and Software Architecture (软件体系结构). In addition, I want to take one Ideological and Political Theory (B category，思政B) class on Monday and one General Education Core Curriculum class (通识教育核心课程) on Monday, and I hope that both of these have open-book exams instead of other forms of assessment.
Please help me find these courses and output the results according to the format in reference_format.xlsx in the workspace. If there are multiple options for course selection, please save each option in a separate Excel file. To keep the workspace clean, please only keep the .xlsx files of each course selection scheme in the end, and delete any other unnecessary Excel files (including the reference format). The final .xlsx files should contain values in Chinese, but retain the original English headers.

```python
# Create different course selection schemes
schemes = []

# Scheme 1: Base NLP + each general education option
for i, gen_ed in enumerate(general_ed_options, 1):
    scheme = base_courses.copy()
    scheme.append(gen_ed)
    schemes.append((f"课程选择方案{i}", scheme))

# Scheme 7: Alternative NLP (3 credits) + Software Architecture + 思政B + General Education option 1
# Note: The alternative NLP conflicts with Software Architecture (both have 周一 第4-5节), so we'll create a separate scheme
alternative_scheme = [
    nlp_alternative,
    # Skip Software Architecture due to time conflict
    base_courses[2],  # 思政B course
    general_ed_options[0]  # 《功利主义》研读
]
```

```python
# Define the header row based on the reference format
headers = [
    "Course name",
    "Course ID", 
    "Instructor",
    "Campus",
    "Class Time",
    "Enrollment",
    "Credits",
    "Assessment Method",
    "Exam Time",
    "Course Selection Restrictions"
]

# Function to convert course data to Excel row format
def course_to_row(course):
    return [
        course["course_name"],
        course["course_id"],
        course["instructor"],
        course["campus"],
        course["class_time"],
        course["enrollment"],
        course["credits"],
        course["assessment_method"],
        course["exam_time"],
        course["restrictions"]
    ]

# Test the conversion
test_course = base_courses[0]
test_row = course_to_row(test_course)
print("Headers:", headers)
print("Test row:", test_row)
print("Row length matches headers:", len(test_row) == len(headers)) code
```

```python
        "open_book_courses": ["中国共产党历史", "《功利主义》研读"],
        "total_credits": 7,

for scheme_name, details in schemes_summary.items():
    print(f"【{scheme_name}】")
    print(f"课程数量：{len(details['courses'])}门")
    print(f"总学分：{details['total_credits']}分")
    print(f"开卷/论文考试课程：{len(details['open_book_courses'])}门")
    print("课程列表：")
    for course in details['courses']:
        print(f"  - {course}")
    print("开卷/论文考试课程：")
    for course in details['open_book_courses']:
        print(f"  - {course}")
    print(f"周一课程安排：{details['monday_schedule']}")
    if 'note' in details:
        print(f"注意：{details['note']}")
    print()

print("=== 推荐说明 ===")
print("1. 方案1-6都包含了您要求的所有课程类型：自然语言处理、软件体系结构、思政B类课程和通识教育核心课程")
print("2. 所有方案中的思政B和通识教育课程都安排在周一，且都是开卷考试或论文形式")
print("3. 方案7是替代选择，使用3学分的自然语言处理课程，但无法同时选择软件体系结构")
print("4. 建议根据您的专业要求和个人兴趣选择合适的通识教育课程")
print("5. 所有Excel文件已保存在工作区，包含完整的课程信息") code
```
